{: .only-website }
  *This is a work in progress jointly with Marc Bezem. Some of
  the following proofs are collapsed or hidden to reduce the size of the document.
  Nevertheless, the reader can click on them to open the full description.
  Pictures are also clickable.*

In this entry, we want to show some equivalences
between the circle and other higher inductive types.

{% comment %}

{: .equation }

  $$\sum\,{\mathbb{S}^1}\,(\mathsf{rec}_{\mathbb{S}^1}\, \mathcal{U}\,  2\,
  (\mathsf{ua}(\mathsf{rec}_{2}2 1_{2} 0_{2}))) \simeq \mathbb{S}^1.$$

Using the flattening lemma we can prove this equivalence:

- [**Direct link PDF**](https://github.com/jonaprieto/flattenlem/files/2045561/Jonathan-Prieto-Cubides-The-Flattening-Lemma.pdf)

{% endcomment %}

<a id="1253" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="1260" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}" class="Module">_</a> <a id="1262" class="Keyword">where</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

##  `S¹` type

The circle is the higher inductive type with one point and one no trivial path
called *path* as we can see in the following picture.

![path](/assets/ipe-images/circle.png){: width="%30" }
*Figure 1. The circle type `S¹`.*

Induction principle on paths:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="2723" class="Comment">-- Postulate.</a>
  <a id="2739" class="Keyword">postulate</a>

## `pS` type

The `pS` type as the figure below shows, it is a circle with two edges
in opposite direction between two points. Notice this HIT is just different
form the suspension of booleans (Σ 2) by reversing one arrow.

![path](/assets/ipe-images/tour-type.png){: width="%40" }
*Figure 2. `pS` Type.*

## `S¹ ≃ pS`

**Lemma 1** . $$ \mathsf{S}^{1} \simeq \mathsf{pS}. $$

**Proof**. We proceed as usual. Defining the outgoing functions and proving
the homotopies. We prove the equivalence by quasiinverse equivalence.

Let `p₀₀` be the path defined as follows. We want to correspond this path with
the `loop` path in order to show the equivalence.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="p₀₀"></a><a id="5864" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#5864" class="Function">p₀₀</a> <a id="5868" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5870" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#3495" class="Function">pS₀</a> <a id="5874" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#6009" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="5877" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#3495" class="Function">pS₀</a>

####  `f ∘ g ~ id`

To prove the homotopy $$ f ∘ g \sim \mathsf{id}$$,
we prove for the pS₁ case and the case for paths.

- Case on `pS₁`:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="6287" class="Comment">-- Def.</a>

    <a id="9502" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#9107" class="Function Operator">∎</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Finally, by path induction on `pS` type, we got the homotopy.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="9594" class="Comment">-- Homotopy.</a>
  <a id="Lemma₁.H₁"></a><a id="9609" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#9609" class="Function">H₁</a> <a id="9612" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9614" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#5982" class="Function">f</a> <a id="9616" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#4135" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="9618" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#6061" class="Function">g</a> <a id="9620" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#28764" class="Function Operator">∼</a> <a id="9622" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3614" class="Function">id</a>
  <a id="9627" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#9609" class="Function">H₁</a> <a id="9630" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9632" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#4530" class="Function">pS-ind</a> <a id="9639" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="9641" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9642" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#6189" class="Function">refl</a> <a id="9647" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#3495" class="Function">pS₀</a><a id="9650" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9652" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#6297" class="Function">q₁</a> <a id="9655" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#6424" class="Function">dpath₀</a> <a id="9662" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#7890" class="Function">dpath₁</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

####  g ∘ f ~ id

To prove this homotopy $$g ∘ f \sim \mathsf{id}$$, we proceed by induction on
the circle. For the `base` case, `refl base` works since `g (f base)` is
definitionally equal to `base`.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="9898" class="Comment">-- Def.</a>
  <a id="Lemma₁.H₂-base"></a><a id="9908" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#9908" class="Function">H₂-base</a> <a id="9916" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="9918" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#1697" class="Function">base</a> <a id="9923" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#6009" class="Datatype Operator">==</a> <a id="9926" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#1697" class="Function">base</a>
  <a id="9933" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#9908" class="Function">H₂-base</a> <a id="9941" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="9943" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#6189" class="Function">refl</a> <a id="9948" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#1697" class="Function">base</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

The rest is how we prove the case for action on `loop`.

We will need the term `aux-path` which is:

{: .foldable until="2"}

{: .foldable until="2" }
<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="10433" class="Comment">-- Def.</a>

## Action on paths of pairs

Action on paths of pairs appears as Lemma 6.12.7 in {% cite hottbook %}.

Let's define out context for this lemma:

And this lemma says:

<a id="13513" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="13518" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#12292" class="Module">Lemma₂</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

##  Σ S¹ P ≃ pS

**Lemma 3.** $$ \Sigma~S^{1}~P~\simeq~pS $$ where
$$P (\mathsf{base}) :≡ \mathsf{Bool}$$ and $$\mathsf{ap~P~loop~=~ua~(neg)}$$.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="13696" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="Lemma₃"></a><a id="13703" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13703" class="Module">Lemma₃</a> <a id="13710" class="Keyword">where</a>

<a id="13717" class="Comment">-- Def.</a>

<a id="neg-eq"></a><a id="13779" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13779" class="Function">neg-eq</a> <a id="13786" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13788" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3086" class="Datatype">Bool</a> <a id="13793" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#33341" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="13795" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3086" class="Datatype">Bool</a>
<a id="13800" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13779" class="Function">neg-eq</a> <a id="13807" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13809" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#48607" class="Function">qinv-≃</a> <a id="13816" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13725" class="Function">neg</a> <a id="13820" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="13821" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13725" class="Function">neg</a> <a id="13825" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#2260" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="13827" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13846" class="Function">h</a> <a id="13829" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#2260" class="InductiveConstructor Operator">,</a> <a id="13831" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13846" class="Function">h</a><a id="13832" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="13836" class="Keyword">where</a>
    <a id="13846" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13846" class="Function">h</a> <a id="13848" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="13850" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13725" class="Function">neg</a> <a id="13854" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#4135" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="13856" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13725" class="Function">neg</a> <a id="13860" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#28764" class="Function Operator">∼</a> <a id="13862" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3614" class="Function">id</a>

    <a id="13887" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13846" class="Function">h</a> <a id="13889" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3122" class="InductiveConstructor">false</a> <a id="13895" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="13897" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#6063" class="InductiveConstructor">idp</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Now, using the negation function as an equivalence, we define the family of types `P`
over the circle S¹.

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="P"></a><a id="14033" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#14033" class="Function">P</a> <a id="14035" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="14037" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#1672" class="Function">S¹</a> <a id="14040" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="14042" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1023" class="Function">Type₀</a>
<a id="14048" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#14033" class="Function">P</a> <a id="14050" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="14052" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#2048" class="Function">S¹-rec</a> <a id="14059" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#1023" class="Function">Type₀</a> <a id="14065" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#3086" class="Datatype">Bool</a> <a id="14070" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14071" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#53341" class="Function">ua</a> <a id="14074" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#13779" class="Function">neg-eq</a><a id="14080" class="Symbol">)</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

Two auxiliar lemmas for the latter:

### g ∘ f ∼ id

Taking inspiration from Flattening lemma's proof in Section 6
in {% cite hottbook %}, we got the following proof.

Finally, the equivalence:
